â”‚                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  1. In  cases  of  a  obligatory  end  of  service,  the  decision  of  the  â”‚
â”‚  government  authority  shall  be  to terminate the employee's service as    â”‚
â”‚  of the day following the day in which his eligibility or validity, which    â”‚
â”‚  are necessary to carry out the job burdens, are gone, and the government    â”‚
â”‚  authority shall not determine any other date.                               â”‚
â”‚  2. In  cases  of  termination  of  the  service  by  the  government        â”‚
â”‚  authority or upon the  request  of the employee, the government authority   â”‚
â”‚  may determine the date of the end of the service by virtue of the decision  â”‚
â”‚  issued in this regard, provided that it is included in the calculation of   â”‚
â”‚  the service period of the notice period, whether the employee worked        â”‚
â”‚  during it, or was exempted from work during it,  or  paid a notice          â”‚
â”‚  allowance for all or part thereof. Cases of end of service by the           â”‚
â”‚  government authority and/or upon the request of the employee, shall         â”‚
â”‚  include the following:                                                      â”‚

â”‚  ## Article ( 131 ) Date of End of Service                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  1. In  cases  of  a  obligatory  end  of  service,  the  decision  of  the  â”‚
â”‚  government  authority  shall  be  to terminate the employee's service as    â”‚
â”‚  of the day following the day in which his eligibility or validity, which    â”‚
â”‚  are necessary to carry out the job burdens, are gone, and the government    â”‚
â”‚  authority shall not determine any other date.                               â”‚
â”‚  2. In  cases  of  termination  of  the  service  by  the  government        â”‚
â”‚  authority or upon the  request  of the employee, the government authority   â”‚
â”‚  may determine the date of the end of the service by virtue of the decision  â”‚
â”‚  issued in this regard, provided that it is included in the calculation of   â”‚
â”‚  the service period of the notice period, whether the employee worked        â”‚
â”‚  during it, or was exempted from work during it,  or  paid a notice          â”‚
â”‚  allowance for all or part thereof. Cases of end of service by the           â”‚
â”‚  government authority and/or upon the request of the employee, shall         â”‚
â”‚  include the following:                                                      â”‚
â”‚  3. AFailing the test period successfully.                                   â”‚
â”‚  4. BThe explicit resignation submitted by the employee.                     â”‚
â”‚  5. CThe  final  ruling  on  the  employee  with  a  sanction  restricted    â”‚
â”‚  to  freedom  in  a  felony  or misdemeanour that violates honour or         â”‚

â”‚  For a non-citizen employee with 12 years of service, the end-of-service     â”‚
â”‚  gratuity is calculated as follows: for the first five years, one month's    â”‚
â”‚  salary; for the next five years, one and a half month's salary; and for     â”‚
â”‚  any years exceeding that, two months' salary.                               â”‚

â”‚  amounts exceed (25%) of the employee's total salary. As an exception, the   â”‚

â”‚  ## Article ( 95 ) Hajj Leave                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  1. A Muslim employee shall be granted a Hajj leave with a total salary to   â”‚
â”‚  perform the Hajj pilgrimage once during their service in the government.    â”‚
â”‚  2. The Hajj leave shall be authorized for a period of (15) working days.    â”‚
â”‚  3. This leave shall be counted within the employee's service period and     â”‚
â”‚  granting it does not affect their annual periodic leave entitlement.        â”‚
â”‚  4. If the employee decided not to take a Hajj leave, such leave shall not   â”‚
â”‚  be considered an acquired right for them, and shall not be included in      â”‚
â”‚  calculating the accrual periodic leave balance at the end of their          â”‚
â”‚  service.                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  5. Upon their return, the employee shall submit documents proving his       â”‚
â”‚  performance of the Hajj during the leave period.                            â”‚
â”‚  6. The total salary of the employee for this leave may be paid in advance   â”‚
â”‚  at their request, provided that the request is made (15) days before the    â”‚
â”‚  start date of their leave.                                                  â”‚

â”‚  ## Article ( 95 ) Hajj Leave                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  1. A Muslim employee shall be granted a Hajj leave with a total salary to   â”‚
â”‚  perform the Hajj pilgrimage once during their service in the government.    â”‚
â”‚  2. The Hajj leave shall be authorized for a period of (15) working days.    â”‚
â”‚  3. This leave shall be counted within the employee's service period and     â”‚
â”‚  granting it does not affect their annual periodic leave entitlement.        â”‚
â”‚  4. If the employee decided not to take a Hajj leave, such leave shall not   â”‚
â”‚  be considered an acquired right for them, and shall not be included in      â”‚
â”‚  calculating the accrual periodic leave balance at the end of their          â”‚
â”‚  service.                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  5. Upon their return, the employee shall submit documents proving his       â”‚
â”‚  performance of the Hajj during the leave period.                            â”‚
â”‚  6. The total salary of the employee for this leave may be paid in advance   â”‚
â”‚  at their request, provided that the request is made (15) days before the    â”‚
â”‚  start date of their leave.                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                              â”‚
